FACILITY   (LINAC,1USALAS)Experiment performed at white neutron   14244  1   17 
           source of the Lujan Center, based on spallation        14244  1   18 
           reactions on a tungsten target using a pulsed          14244  1   19 
           800-MeV proton beam, accumulated in the proton         14244  1   20 
           storage ring.                                          14244  1   21 
DETECTOR   (BAF2) 4PI gamma-detector array DANCE, composed of     14244  1   22 
           160 BaF2 scintillators.DANCE provides the total        14244  1   23 
           g-ray calorimetry and the multiplicity information     14244  1   24 
           of the g-cascade following neutron capture. DANCE is   14244  1   25 
           located on a 20 m flight path.                         14244  1   26 
METHOD     (TOF) Incident neutron energy determined by time of    14244  1   27 
           flight. Proton beam was compressed to a 250 ns pulse   14244  1   28 
           and delivered into tungsten spallation target at a     14244  1   29 
           repetition rate of 20 Hz. DANCE array was located on   14244  1   30 
           a 20.25 m long flight path.                            14244  1   31 
MONITOR    (5-B-10(N,A)3-LI-7,,SIG) The monitor was a BF3         14244  1   32 
           ionization chamber. Both reaction products were        14244  1   33 
           detected.)                                             14244  1   34 
MONIT-REF  (,S.F.Mughabghab,B,NEUT.RES,,71-9,2006) S.F.Mughabghab,14244  1   35 
            Atlas of Neutron Resonances, Elsevier (2006).         14244  1   36 
INC-SOURCE (SPALL) Pulsed 800-MeV proton beam impinging on W      14244  1   37 
           target. The bunch length was 200 ns and the            14244  1   38 
           repetition rate 20 Hz. Sample and detector placed at   14244  1   39 
           a distance of 20 m.                                    14244  1   40
